GT: c0*(c1 - P/c2)*P + c3*P**c4 + c5*P*exp(-c6*t)
Candidate formulas: 50

Let  
\[
\text{GT}(t,P)=0.7124493718672418\Big(1-\frac{P}{68.90600928530216}\Big)P\;+\;0.7124493718672418\,P^{1/3}\;+\;0.7124493718672418\,P\,e^{-0.03459335742983884\,t}.
\]
Key structural facts about GT:

- It is a sum of **three** terms: a **quadratic polynomial in \(P\)** (no \(t\)), plus a **fractional power** \(P^{1/3}\) (no \(t\)), plus a **separable term** \(P\cdot e^{kt}\) with \(k\neq 0\).
- There are **no** terms like \(e^{P\cdot(\cdot)}\), \(\log(\cdot)\), \(\sin\), \(\tanh\), rational-in-\(t\) factors like \(1/(c+t)\), etc.
- The only \(t\)-dependence is exactly \(P\cdot e^{kt}\) with \(k=-0.03459...\).

So any matching candidate must be able (by parameter choice) to produce simultaneously:
1) a \(P^2\) term and a \(P\) term with **no \(t\)**,  
2) a \(P^{1/3}\) term with **no \(t\)**,  
3) a \(P e^{kt}\) term with \(k\neq 0\),  
and must avoid introducing any other functional dependence (like \(e^{P c}\), logs, trig, \(t\)-polynomials, denominators in \(t\), etc.) unless they can be identically removed by setting coefficients to 0.

Now check each candidate.

1. \(P^2 c0 e^{c1 t} + P c2 e^{P c3} + P c4 e^{c5 t} + c6 + c7 e^{c8 t}/P^5\)  
   Has \(e^{P c3}\) unless \(c2=0\). Also has constant \(c6\) and \(P^{-5}\) term unless set to 0. Even after zeroing those, remaining terms are \(P^2 e^{c1 t}\) and \(P e^{c5 t}\). GT needs \(P^2\) with **no \(t\)** and also a separate \(P e^{kt}\) plus \(P^{1/3}\). No way to get \(P^{1/3}\). **No match.**

2. \(P c0 e^{c1 t} + P^{c2} c3 + P^{c4} c5 e^{c6 t} + c7 t e^{c8 t} + c9\)

But still need the quadratic polynomial \(aP-bP^2\) with no \(t\). The only remaining term \(P^{c4} c5 e^{c6 t}\) cannot produce simultaneously \(P\) and \(P^2\) without \(t\) (it’s a single monomial times possibly an exponential). If set \(c6=0\), it becomes one monomial \(c5 P^{c4}\), not a sum of \(P\) and \(P^2\). **No match.**

Expanding: `0.7124*P - 0.01034*P² + 0.7124*P^(1/3) + 0.7124*P*exp(-0.03459*t)`

The GT has these basis functions:
1. `P²` (with constant coefficient)
2. `P` (with constant coefficient)
3. `P^(1/3)` (with constant coefficient)
4. `P*exp(-c*t)` (with constant coefficient, c > 0)

### Candidate 5:
`P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + P*c3 + P^c4*P^c5*c6 + P^c4*c7 + c8*t*exp(c9*t)`

Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 14:
`P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + P^c4*c5*exp(c6*t) + c7 + c8*exp(c9*t)`

Result: `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + c5*P^(1/3)`

This matches GT! Set c0=-0.01034, c1=0.7124, c2=0.7124, c3=-0.03459, c4=1/3, c5=0.7124, c6=0, c7=0, c8=0.

### Candidate 42:
